<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подавить.html>подави́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podavítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подавиться.html>подави́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podavítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давиться.html>дави́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to choke <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">be unable to breathe because of obstruction of the windpipe</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подавить.html>подави́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podavítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подавление.html>подавле́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podavlénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подавление.html>подавле́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подавление.html>подавле́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подавление.html>подавле́ний</a></b>)

***подавлять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подавлять.html>подавля́ть</a> (4771)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подавить.html>подави́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podavítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подавлять.html>подавля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podavljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подавить.html>подави́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to suppress, to repress, to quell, to stifle</li>
<li>to depress, to overwhelm</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подавлять.html>подавля́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podavljájuščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подавлять.html>подавля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podavljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подавлять.html>подавля́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podavljájuščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>overwhelming
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подавляющий.html>подавля́ющее</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:большинство.html>большинство́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podavljájuščeje</b> bolʹšinstvó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">overwhelming majority</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>depressing</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подавно.html>пода́вно</a> (14971)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:годиться.html>гожу́сь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:подавно.html>пода́вно</a></strong></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ja na éto ne gožúsʹ, a ty i podávno</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I am not fit for that, and you even less so</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дар.html>дар</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dar</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ок</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подарок.html>пода́рок</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podárok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подарок.html>пода́рка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подарок.html>пода́рки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подарок.html>пода́рков</a></b>)

<ol><li>present, gift
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:какой.html>како́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хо́чешь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подарок.html>пода́рок</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kakój xóčešʹ <b>podárok</b>?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">What do you want as <b>a present</b>?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***подать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подать.html>подать</a> (4380)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">datʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подать.html>пода́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подавать.html>подава́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to give, to proffer, to pass
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подать.html>пода́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podátʹ</b> rúku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to offer one's hand</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подать.html>пода́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сигнал.html>сигна́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podátʹ</b> signál</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give the signal</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подать.html>пода́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:надежда.html>наде́жду</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podátʹ</b> nadéždu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give hope</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to serve
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подать.html>пода́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>стол</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podátʹ</b> na stol</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to serve up</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pitch, to serve, to pass
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>Из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:боковой.html>боково́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:позиция.html>пози́ции</a> пи́тчер <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подать.html>пода́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мяч.html>мяч</a> бэ́ттеру, <a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сде́лать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:передача.html>переда́чу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:база.html>ба́зу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>и́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сойти.html>сойти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пластина.html>пласти́ны</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Iz bokovój pozícii pítčer móžet <b>podátʹ</b> mjač bɛ́tteru, sdélatʹ peredáču na bázu íli sojtí s plastíny.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">From the set position, the pitcher can pitch the ball to the batter, throw it to a base, or move off the pitching rubber.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to give alms</li></ol>

***подача.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подача.html>пода́ча</a> (8347)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подача.html>пода́ча</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podáča</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подача.html>пода́чи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подача.html>пода́чи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подача.html>пода́ч</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>giving
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбор.html>сбор</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подача.html>пода́чу</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:такси.html>такси́</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sbor za <b>podáču</b> taksí</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">picking-up charge</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подача.html>пода́чи</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s podáči</i> ― <span class="e-translation">1) at the instigation; 2) at the suggestion, on the tip</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подача.html>пода́ча</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голос.html>голоса</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">podáča golosa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">voting</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">technology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> feed, feeding, supply</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> service, serve
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переход.html>перехо́д</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подача.html>пода́чи</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">perexód <b>podáči</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">change of service</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потеря.html>поте́ря</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подача.html>пода́чи</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">potérja <b>podáči</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">loss of service</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подача.html>пода́че</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bytʹ na <b>podáče</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to be serving</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голый.html>гол</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:забитый.html>заби́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подача.html>пода́чи</a></b> Н.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gol byl zabit s <b>podáči</b> N.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">N. assisted in scoring</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>presentation, portrayal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">необъективная <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подача.html>пода́ча</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:факт.html>фа́ктов</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">neobʺjektivnaja <b>podáča</b> fáktov</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">biased/unfair presentation of facts</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подача.html>пода́ча</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podáča</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подачка.html>пода́чка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podáčka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подачка.html>пода́чки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подачка.html>пода́чки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подачка.html>пода́чек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pittance, dole, charity, sop, tip (also figuratively)</li></ol>

***подбегать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подбегать.html>подбега́ть</a> (10142)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бегать.html>бе́гать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bégatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подбегать.html>подбега́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podbegátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подбежать.html>подбежа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to run up, to come running up to</li></ol>

***подбивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подбивать.html>подбива́ть</a> (18935)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подбить.html>подби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podbítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подбивать.html>подбива́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podbivátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подбить.html>подби́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to line (lining)</li>
<li>to resole (shoes)</li>
<li>to damage, to hurt (e.g. a person's eye)</li>
<li>to shoot down (bird, airplane)</li>
<li>to instigate, to abet <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to assist or encourage in crime</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to assess, to sum up, to reckon up</li></ol>

***подбирать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подбирать.html>подбира́ть</a> (5603)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-бира́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-birátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подбирать.html>подбира́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podbirátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подобрать.html>подобра́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pick up</li>
<li>to sort out, to select, to glean</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подбираться.html>подбира́ться</a> (10348)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подбирать.html>подбира́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podbirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подбираться.html>подбира́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podbirátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подобраться.html>подобра́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to form</li>
<li>to steal up <i>(to)</i>, to approach stealthily</li>
<li>to find an approach <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:давно.html>давно́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>ней</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подбираться.html>подбира́юсь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ja davnó k nej <b>podbirájusʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">I've long been trying to contact [find an approach to] her</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to aim <i>(for)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подбираться.html>подбира́ется</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>моему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>podbirájetsja</b> k mojemú méstu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he aims for my job</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to tuck, to crouch</li>
<li>to straighten oneself up</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подбирать.html>подбира́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podbirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подбирать.html>подбира́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podbirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подобрать.html>подобра́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podobrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подобранный.html>подо́бранный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podóbrannyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подбирающий.html>подбира́ющий</a> (5603)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подбирающий.html>подбира́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podbirájuščij</span>)
</p>
